## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kafka Inter-Broker Replication Protocol Architecture

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in apache/kafka that implement the inter-broker replication protocol: the ReplicaFetcherThread, the LeaderEpochFileCache, the LogStartOffset tracking, and the ISR (in-sync replica) shrink/expand mechanism.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the org domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.

```json

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Kafka Inter-Broker Replication Protocol Files

### ReplicaFetcherThread
- **`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaFetcherThread.scala`** — Main follower-side replication thread; fetches from leader, tracks `logStartOffset`, handles truncation
- **`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/AbstractFetcherThread.scala`** — Base class with core fetch loop, truncation logic, and abstract `logStartOffset()` method
- **`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/AbstractFetcherManager.scala`** — Abstract manager maintaining a pool of fetcher threads
- **`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaFetcherManager.scala`** — Creates `ReplicaFetcherThread` instances with `RemoteLeaderEndPoint`
- **`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/RemoteLeaderEndPoint.scala`** — Leader endpoint for fetching from remote brokers via Kafka wire protocol
- **`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/LocalLeaderEndPoint.scala`** — Leader endpoint for local log directory alterations
- **`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaAlterLogDirsThread.scala`** — Sibling fetcher for cross-directory log replication
- **`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaAlterLogDirsManager.scala`** — Manager for alter-log-dirs threads

### LeaderEpochFileCache
- **`storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/epoch/LeaderEpochFileCache.java`** — Main implementation mapping epochs to start offsets
- **`storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/LeaderEpochCheckpointFile.java`** — File-backed persistence for epoch data
- **`storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/EpochEntry.java`** — Data class for epoch-to-offset entries

`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaFetcherThread.scala`: The main follower-side thread that fetches data from the leader broker. It overrides `logStartOffset()` to return the local replica's log start offset, and calls `log.maybeIncrementLogStartOffset()` with `LogStartOffsetIncrementReason.LeaderOffsetIncremented` when the leader's log start offset advances.\\n- `core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/AbstractFetcherThread.scala`: The abstract base class containing the core fetch loop logic, truncation logic (`getOffsetTruncationState`), and the abstract `logStartOffset()` method.\\n- `core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/AbstractFetcherManager.scala`: Abstract manager that maintains a pool of fetcher threads keyed by (fetcherId, sourceBroker).\\n- `core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaFetcherManager.scala`: Concrete manager that creates `ReplicaFetcherThread` instances, wiring them with `RemoteLeaderEndPoint`.\\n- `core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/RemoteLeaderEndPoint.scala`: Implements the `LeaderEndPoint` interface for fetching from a remote broker via the Kafka wire protocol (blocking network sends).\\n- `core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/LocalLeaderEndPoint.scala`: Implements `LeaderEndPoint` for local log directory alterations.\\n- `core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaAlterLogDirsThread.scala`: A sibling fetcher thread for cross-directory log replication (future log).\\n- `core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaAlterLogDirsManager.scala`: Manager for `ReplicaAlterLogDirsThread` instances.\\n\\n## LeaderEpochFileCache\\n\\n- `storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/epoch/LeaderEpochFileCache.java`: The main implementation of the leader epoch cache. It maintains a mapping of leader epochs to their start offsets, persisted via `LeaderEpochCheckpointFile`. Used during truncation to determine the correct offset to truncate to when a follower reconnects after a leader change.\\n- `storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/LeaderEpochCheckpointFile.java`: The file-backed checkpoint that persists epoch-to-offset mappings to disk (in the `leader-epoch-checkpoint` file in each log directory).\\n- `storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/EpochEntry.java`: Data class representing a single epoch-to-startOffset mapping entry.\\n\\n## LogStartOffset Tracking\\n\\n- `storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/UnifiedLog.java`: The unified log abstraction that holds `logStartOffset` and `localLogStartOffset` as volatile fields. Provides `maybeIncrementLogStartOffset()` and `maybeIncrementLocalLogStartOffset()` methods used by the replication protocol to advance the follower's log start offset when the leader's advances.\\n- `storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogStartOffsetIncrementReason.java`: Enum enumerating reasons for log start offset increments: `LeaderOffsetIncremented`, `SegmentDeletion`, `ClientRecordDeletion`, `SnapshotGenerated`.\\n- `storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogLoader.java`: Loads and recovers log segments on startup, using `LeaderEpochFileCache` to rebuild epoch state.\\n- `storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LocalLog.java`: The lower-level local log implementation managing segments, recovery points, and flush state.\\n- `storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogSegment.java`: Individual log segment with a `recover()` method that accepts a `LeaderEpochFileCache` to rebuild epoch entries during recovery.\\n\\n## ISR Shrink/Expand Mechanism\\n\\n- `core/src/main/scala/kafka/cluster/Partition.scala`: The central class implementing ISR management. Contains `maybeShrinkIsr()` (checks if any replicas have fallen behind and initiates shrink), `maybeExpandIsr()` (called after a follower fetch to check if it has caught up and should be added to ISR), and the state classes `PendingShrinkIsr` and `PendingExpandIsr` for tracking in-flight AlterPartition requests. Also defines the `AlterPartitionListener` trait for ISR change notifications.\\n- `core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaManager.scala`: Schedules the periodic `isr-expiration` task that calls `maybeShrinkIsr()` on all partitions. Tracks ISR expand/shrink/failure metrics (`IsrExpandsPerSec`, `IsrShrinksPerSec`, `FailedIsrUpdatesPerSec`).\\n- `core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/AlterPartitionManager.scala`: Manages the submission of ISR change requests to the controller via `AlterPartition` API. The `DefaultAlterPartitionManager` batches and retries these requests.\\n\\n## Supporting Files\\n- `core/src/main/java/kafka/server/TierStateMachine.java`: Handles tiered storage state transitions, reading `LeaderEpochCheckpointFile` data from remote storage to rebuild epoch caches when a follower needs to fetch from tiered storage.\"\n}\n",
